ind. (+imp) please!; come on!; go on!; move it!; check it out! [√iñj + a] ✓

Examples

icc

Construction iti > ity > icc

Sanskrit iti

Examples

Meaning wishing for; desiring; wanting
Root Family √is

Examples

nt. movement; perturbation; agitation; turmoil; disturbance; lit. moved [√iñj + ita] ✓

Grammar nt, pp of iñjati
Meaning movement; perturbation; agitation; turmoil; disturbance; lit. moved
Root Family √iñj
Root √iñj･1 a (move, shake)
Construction √iñj + ita
Derivative kita (ita)
Antonym aniñjita
Synonym iñjitatta
Commentary (ANa) iñjitan'ti rāg'iñjitaṃ dosa-moha-māna-diṭṭhi-kilesa-duccarit'iñjitan'ti imāni satta iñjitāni calitāni phanditāni.
Sanskrit iṅgita
Sanskrit Root √iṅg 1 (stir)

Examples

ākāse'va padaṃ n'atthi,
samaṇo n'atthi bāhire,
saṅkhārā sassatā n'atthi,
n'atthi buddhānam'iñjitaṃ.

DHP 255 malavaggo

saṅkhāya lokasmi paroparāni,
yass'iñjitaṃ n'atthi kuhiñci loke,
santo vidhūmo anīgho nirāso,
atāri so jātijaran'ti brūmī'ti.

Grammar idiom, adv + ind + ind

Sanskrit iti + vā + hi

Example

MN 25 nivāpasuttaṃ
itibhavābhava

masc. this or that state of existence [iti + bhava + abhava] ✓

Grammar masc, abstr, comp
Meaning this or that state of existence
Construction iti + bhava + abhava
Compound dvanda (itibhava vā abhava vā)
Sanskrit iti + bhavābhava

Examples

na kho pan'āhaṃ cīvarahetu agārasmā anagāriyaṃ pabbajito. na piṇḍapātahetu, na sen'āsanahetu, na itibhav'ābhavahetu agārasmā anagāriyaṃ pabbajito.

AN 3.40 ādhipateyyasuttaṃ

itthikathaṃ sūrakathaṃ visikhākathaṃ kumbhaṭṭhānakathaṃ pubbapetakathaṃ nānattakathaṃ lok'akkhāyikaṃ samudd'akkhāyikaṃ itibhav'ābhavakathaṃ iti vāti

AN 10.69 paṭhamakathāvatthusuttaṃ
itibhavābhavakathā

fem. such talk about existence or non-existence; discussion about this or that state of existence [iti + bhava + abhava + kathā] ✓

Grammar fem, comp
Meaning such talk about existence or non-existence; discussion about this or that state of existence
Construction iti + bhava + abhava + kathā
Compound chaṭṭhī tappurisa (itibhavābhavassa + kathā)
Sanskrit iti + bhavābhava + kathā

Example

itthikathaṃ sūrakathaṃ visikhākathaṃ kumbhaṭṭhānakathaṃ pubbapetakathaṃ nānattakathaṃ lok'akkhāyikaṃ samudd'akkhāyikaṃ itibhav'ābhavakathaṃ iti vāti

AN 10.69 paṭhamakathāvatthusuttaṃ
itibhavābhavatā

fem. fact of being (reborn in) any such state of existence; (comm) such success and failure, gain and loss, eternity and annihilation, good and evil [iti + bhava + abhava + tā] ✓

Grammar fem, abstr, comp
Meaning fact of being (reborn in) any such state of existence; (comm) such success and failure, gain and loss, eternity and annihilation, good and evil
Construction iti + bhava + abhava + tā
itibhavābhava + tā
Derivative taddhita (tā)
Commentary (UDa) itibhav'ābhavatañ'ca vītivatto'ti yasmā bhavo'ti sampatti, abhavo'ti vipatti. tathā bhavo'ti vuddhi, abhavoti hāni. bhavo'ti vā sassataṃ, abhavo'ti ucchedo. bhavo'ti vā puññaṃ, abhavo'ti pāpaṃ. (SNPa) tasmā itibhav'ābhavatañ'ca vītivatto'ti ettha yā esā sampatti-vipatti-vuḍḍhi-hāni-sassat'uccheda-puñña-pāpa-vasena iti anekappakārā bhav'ābhavatā vuccati. catūhi'pi maggehi yathāsambhavaṃ tena tena nayena taṃ itibhav'ābhavatañ'ca vītivatto'ti evam'attho ñātabbo.
Sanskrit iti + bhava + abhava +

Example

yass'antarato na san'ti kopā,
itibhav'ābhavatañ'ca vītivatto,
taṃ vigatabhayaṃ sukhiṃ asokaṃ,
devā n'ānubhavanti dassanāyā'ti.

UD 20 bhaddiyasuttaṃ
itibhavābhavahetu

ind. for the sake of this or that state of existence [iti + bhava + abhava + hetu] ✓

Grammar ind, adv, comp
Meaning for the sake of this or that state of existence
Construction iti + bhava + abhava + hetu
Compound chaṭṭhī tappurisa (itibhavābhavassa + hetu)
Commentary (ANa) na iti bhav'ābhavahetū'ti iti bhavo, iti bhavo'ti evaṃ āyatiṃ, na tassa tassa sampattibhavassa hetu.
Sanskrit iti + bhavābhava + hetu

Example

na kho pan'āhaṃ cīvarahetu agārasmā anagāriyaṃ pabbajito. na piṇḍapātahetu, na sen'āsanahetu, na itibhav'ābhavahetu agārasmā anagāriyaṃ pabbajito.

itivādappamokkha

masc. winning debates; refuting ideology; (comm) freeing others from their faulty views [iti + vāda + pamokkha] ✓

Grammar masc, comp
Meaning winning debates; refuting ideology; (comm) freeing others from their faulty views
Construction iti + vāda + pamokkha

Commentary (MNa) itivādappamokkh'ānisaṃsā cā'ti evaṃ vādapamokkh'ānisaṃsā, parehi sakavāde dose āropite taṃ dosaṃ evaṃ mocessāmāti iminā'va kāraṇena pariyāpuṇantī'ti attho. (SNa) itivādappamokkh'ānisaṃsan'ti evaṃ pucchā hoti, evaṃ vissajjanaṃ, evaṃ gahaṇaṃ, evaṃ nibbeṭhanan'ti iminā nayena itivādo hoti itivādappamokkho'ti etaṃ ānisaṃsaṃ.

evam'pi titthyā puthuso vadanti,
sandiṭṭhirāgena hi te'bhirattā.

Examples

Sanskrit īrṣyamāṇa

Example

issāmanikā kho pana hoti, paralābha-sakkāra-garukāra-mānana-vandana-pūjanāsu issati upadussati issaṃ bandhati.
